üõè „ÄêÔ∏èCheck-in Guide for InterContinental Foshan Dongping Poly Hotel„Äë

üìå Hotel Overview Overview

1. Comprehensive evaluation (highlights, shortcomings, regrets): InterContinental Dongping was previously called InterContinental Xincheng, and now it has been renamed Foshan Shunde Dongping Poly Intercontinental Hotel. The direction is clearer, and the name change was successful! I have stayed at this hotel three times before and this is my fourth time. There are now 9 InterContinental hotels in the prefecture-level city of Foshan (two InterContinental brands, two Crowns, two Holiday Inns, and three Smart Select hotels). I have checked in several times. This IC is undoubtedly the best in software and hardware among the nine. Outstanding.

üè® About the room In Room

1. Welcome gift and upgrade benefits (whether the trea**ent is good or not): The hotel upgraded us to a 78-square-meter one-bedroom suite. Due to the scarcity of this room type (because there are many regular guests in the hotel, there are many foreigners in the public areas such as breakfast and gym). You can get a glimpse of the ratio. Many of them are expatriates from high-end companies and live in the suites as apar**ents.), and the occupancy rate is extremely high, it is difficult to squeeze out a room. Thank you. The welcome fruits are extremely rich in variety, including mango, dragon fruit, etc., with good appearance and taste; the welcome snacks include cashew nuts, macadamia nuts, peanuts, etc.
2. Evaluation of guest room layout and hardware (whether the room is big or not): The large round bathtub in the guest room is similar to the suite in Nanhai Holiday. The living room window faces the landmark building: Foshan Grand Theater; the coffee cup in the living room is very exquisite; Dyson hair dryer and capsule coffee machine are standard equipment in the suite. The turndown service was particularly attentive, and the handwritten welcome letter was warm and tender. I would like to thank the family members in the housekeeping depar**ent for making us feel at home again!
3. Minibar and bathroom accessories: All InterContinental hotels under the "Poly" series in Guangdong use separate bathroom accessories (more diluted and warm plant texture), which is different from traditional IHG hotels; this is like Century InterContinental Hotels owned by City Convention and Exhibition (from private to Yunnan Urban Inves**ent, Sunac, and private) all have the word "Paradise" on them. In addition, the bathroom accessories in the InterContinental Suites at Dongping are in portable packaging in small tubes, while the InterContinental at Qiandeng Lake is in environmentally friendly packaging in large tubs.

‚òïÔ∏è Dining

1. Types of meals and services in the executive lounge (like or dislike): The service is not arrogant, but conscientious and well-behaved, giving people a feeling of spring breeze. Barbara and Janice in the front office can be said to be responsive to all requests and have extremely high professionalism. They left a deep impression on me, my wife, and our two sons. With this kind of ability, we are fully qualified even if we go to Six Senses.
2. Hotel breakfast types and services (good or bad): There is a self-service juice pressing area, which is exactly the same as the machine at my home, so my two sons can easily do everything from selecting ingredients to juicing; Diamond Ambassador will have a special dining area. If it is full, We will also help guide you to the relatively private large long table behind the screen on the back. There is an exclusive menu for Diamond Ambassadors, including several types of Starbucks co-branded freshly ground coffee, eggs Benedict, and steamed snacks (shrimp dumplings, siomai, chicken feet, etc.).
3. Hotel restaurant hardware, taste and service: Because it is a Chinese owner, like the Qiandeng Lake InterContinental, it has the famous Royal Mansion. The Chinese restaurant is of first-class quality and is suitable for business banquets.

üèä Hardware facilities Facilities

1. Hotel environment: The two Lingnan lions in the lobby are sensor-activated. Children love to interact with them. The rich Cantonese culture is immersed in the joy, which is really great.
2. Gym and swimming pool (new): InterContinental Qiandeng Lake only has an outdoor swimming pool. InterContinental Dongping, which opened later, learned from experience and has both outdoor and indoor swimming pools. The gym equipment is also updated.
3. Children's play: A banquet hall on the first floor has been transformed into a children's inflatable castle park. In this way, even if it is windy or rainy, children will have a good place to play. This is very similar to Anji Clubmed.

üåü The Moments

1. Highlights (advantages and disadvantages): Even compared with the newly opened Wuxi Taihu Intercontinental, it is comparable. Many small details make us feel that the service of this hotel is particularly sophisticated and unique: a small refrigerator with a display of drinks The neatness of placement, the beauty of paper towel folding in the bathroom and bedroom toilet paper boxes, etc.
      2. Star employees‚Äô outstanding performance and awards (whether the service is strong or not): There are too many things to praise, but due to limited space, let‚Äôs focus on thanking colleagues in the catering depar**ent. When having breakfast, he took the initiative to help me get seated, and also helped me keep ordering the dishes (member food). I thought to myself, if I was in a hurry to catch an early flight, I would be so happy to stay in such an efficient hotel!

üìç Brief summary Conclusion

1. Highlights of the trip: During this business trip, in addition to work, I also took my wife and children to the two-day Strawberry Music Festival. The children met a bunch of rock idols at the venue, hotel, and airport lounge, and they were very happy. Among the 21 prefecture-level cities in Guangdong, Shenzhen, Guangzhou, and Foshan have always ranked first, second, and third in terms of GDP (even on a per capita basis, Foshan ranks second). Therefore, in Foshan you will deeply feel what it means to be wealthy.
2. Surrounding food, attractions, and entertainment: Next to it is the Ascott Apar**ents, and downstairs is a snack street with strong fireworks. Xinjiang's large skewers are particularly authentic. Foshan has 5 districts. Shunde is a well-deserved industrial town and gourmet paradise (there are so many delicious foods, you don‚Äôt necessarily have to go to "Diandu De"). Its popularity even exceeds Foshan itself in many aspects. Nanhai is another cornerstone of Foshan‚Äôs economic development. On one side, Chancheng is the actual central area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe quaint old city, while Gaoming and Sanshui are the outer suburbs. Dongping Intercontinental is located in Dongping New Town, Lecong Town, Shunde District, Foshan City (Shunde has 4 streets and 6 towns) (Lecong has 7 communities and 19 villages, Dongping New Town belongs to Dongping Community).

1‚É£Ô∏èThe epidemic prevention work is worrying. No health code is required to be shown when entering and leaving, and no temperature is measured. It is terrifying to think about it. 2‚É£Ô∏èThe quality of some employees is not up to standard. After entering the lobby, there are only 2 counters to check in, and it takes at least 7 or 8 minutes to handle a customer... There are 3 people in front of us. We arrived at 1 o'clock, and the child was a little restless. I didn't want to affect other hotel staff, so I found the lady in the maroon suit in the lobby to communicate... Her reaction made me speechless... I was almost confused. Is this a five-star hotel? I asked her to communicate with the colleague at the counter where I bought the Rewards Club to see if we could arrange to check in behind that gentleman. She asked me to communicate by myself. After I replied, I reluctantly told the colleague in the concierge department who was wearing blue clothes and gray pants. I didn't expect that it would end in nothing after I talked... The child continued to cry. I had no choice but to find a colleague in the concierge department who I added on WeChat. He asked me to go to the You* Club counter to apply for membership, which was free... This was the solution.
By then, my child had cried like a tearful child. The two eyeless lions in the lobby scared her a lot. Today is the 8th, and she still cried and said don't go out again when she thinks of it. There are scary things outside...
3‚É£Ô∏è The room hygiene is worrying. After checking in at 1421, it was said that it was upgraded to a garden view room. There was no garden inside, only a construction site... There were actually! There were actually food residues left by the previous guest on the table! Is this a five-star hotel? ... I can only find the manager to change our room. 1823, I heard the sound of a water pump at night. I don't know which room it was from. The executive room is like this... Fortunately, I stayed for 1 night, so forget it...
4‚É£Ô∏è The leisure area is not well managed. It is also advertised as a family hotel... I dare not go into the children's play area on the 6th floor! It can accommodate 5 or 6 children, and if there are more parents, it will be like a shopping mall playground on weekends. Who dares to go in...
The outdoor swimming pool is full of second-hand smoke, and unscrupulous smokers flick cigarette butts into the pool. The swimming pool is also pitifully small... The new hotel is planned like this... The country has called for 3 children. How many families can this size accommodate?
The management is too poor...
5‚É£Ô∏è I called the front desk to deliver something. I clearly said "please do not disturb", but they still disturbed me...
